9b6(1): bsnams// g.yon na thod khrag zhal du gsol// g.yon na dpal ldan re ma ti// sku mdog dmar nag ral pa can// g.yas pa bdud kyi khram pam bsnams// g.yon na nad kyi stsal pa 'dzin//
